## Example 20.1


### (a),(b)



```python
DATA ex20_1;
	input X1 X2 X3 X4 X5 @@;
	cards;
6 9.9 5.7 1.6 2.12
1 9.3 6.4 3 3.39
-2 9.4 5.7 3.4 3.61
11 9.1 6.1 3.4 1.72
-1 6.9 6 3 1.8
2 9.3 5.7 4.4 3.21
5 7.9 5.9 2.2 2.59
1 7.4 6.2 2.2 3.25
1 7.3 5.5 1.9 2.86
3 8.8 5.2 0.2 2.32
11 9.8 5.7 4.2 1.57
9 10.5 6.1 2.4 1.5
5 9.1 6.4 3.4 2.69
-3 10.1 5.5 3 4.06
1 7.2 5.5 0.2 1.98
8 11.7 6 3.9 2.29
-2 8.7 5.5 2.2 3.55
3 7.6 6.2 4.4 3.31
6 8.6 5.9 0.2 1.83
10 10.9 5.6 2.4 1.69
4 7.6 5.8 2.4 2.42
5 7.3 5.8 4.4 2.98
5 9.2 5.2 1.6 1.84
3 7 6 1.9 2.48
8 7.2 5.5 1.6 2.83
8 7 6.4 4.1 2.41
6 8.8 6.2 1.9 1.78
6 10.1 5.4 2.2 2.22
3 12.1 5.4 4.1 2.72
5 7.7 6.2 1.6 2.36
1 7.8 6.8 2.4 2.81
8 11.5 6.2 1.9 1.64
10 10.4 6.4 2.2 1.82
;run;

proc corr data=ex20_1 nosimple; 
var X1 X2 X3 X4 X5;
run;
```

### (c)



```python
proc glmselect data=ex20_1;
	model X5 = X1 X2 X3 X4  / selection=none stb showpvalues; 
	ods select ParameterEstimates;
```

### (d)



```python
ods graphics off; ods exclude all; ods noresults;
proc glm data=ex20_1;
	model X5 = X1 X2 X3 X4; 
	ods output OverallANOVA=OverallANOVA2
						FitStatistics=FitStatistics;
RUN ;
ods graphics on; ods exclude none; ods results;
proc print data=OverallANOVA2 label;
run;
```

```python
data FitStatistics_20;
set FitStatistics;
adj_Rsquare = 1 - ((1 - RSquare)*((33 - 1) / (33 - 4 - 1)));
R = sqrt(RSquare);
label adj_Rsquare  = "Adj R-Square";
run;
proc print data=FitStatistics_20 label;
var RSquare adj_Rsquare R RootMSE;
run;
```

```python
	model X5 = X1 X2 X3 X4;
```

### (e)



```python
ods html;
ods graphics on;
proc glmselect data=ex20_1 ;
	model X5 = X1 X2 X3 X4  / selection=backward stb showpvalues details=all stats=all; 
RUN ;
ods graphics off;
ods html close;
```

## Example 20.2



```python
proc factor data=ex20_1 MSA;
	ods select ParCorrControlVar;
run;
```

## Example 20.3



```python
DATA A;
	INPUT X1 X4;
	DATALINES;
		7 2
		;
RUN;

DATA e_203;
set a ex20_1;
run;

ods graphics off; ods exclude all; ods noresults;
PROC REG data=e_203;
 model x5=x1 x4 / p clm cli;
ods output OutputStatistics=OutputStatistics;
run;
ods graphics on; ods exclude none; ods results;

proc print data=OutputStatistics label;
run;
```

## Example 20.4



```python
proc iml;
	reset nolog;
	sst=1577.3106;
	ssp=1298.4789;
	m=4;
	k=3;
	f=round(((sst-ssp)/((m+1)*(k-1)))/(ssp/111) , 0.01); 
	p=round(1-probf(f, 10, 111), 0.001);
	print f p ;
RUN;
```

## Example 20.5



```python
DATA e_205 ; 
input variable bird rank @@ ;
datalines ; 
1 1 4 1 2 8.5 1 3 10 1 4 1.5 1 5 3 1 6 1.5 1 7 7 1 8 5 
1 9 8.5 1 10 11 1 11 6 1 12 12
2 1 5 2 2 7 2 3 11 2 4 2.5 2 5 5 2 6 1 2 7 5 2 8 2.5 2 
9 9.5 2 10 8 2 11 9.5 2 12 12
3 1 5.5 3 2 5.5 3 3 9.5 3 4 2 3 5 3 3 6 1 3 7 8 3 8 4 3 
9 11 3 10 9.5 3 11 7 3 12 12
;
run;

proc freq data=e_205;
 	table variable*bird*rank / noprint cmh scores=rank;;
run;
```

## Example 20.6



```python
DATA e_206;
	input girl flavor $  preference @@ ; 
	datalines ; 
1 cc 5 1 c 1 1 s 3 1 v 2 1 bp 4 1 n 6
2 cc 6 2 c 2 2 s 3 2 v 1 2 bp 5 2 n 4
3 cc 6 3 c 3 3 s 2 3 v 1 3 bp 4 3 n 5
;
run;

PROC FREQ data=e_206;
	tables girl*flavor*preference / noprint cmh scores=rank;
run;
```

## Example 20.7



```python
ods graphics off; ods exclude all; ods noresults;
proc npar1way savage data=e_206 ; 
class flavor ; 
var preference ;
exact ; 
ods output SavageAnalysis=SavageAnalysis;
run ; 
ods graphics on; ods exclude none; ods results;

PROC PRINT DATA=SavageAnalysis;
RUN;
```
